	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">En l&aelig;rende organisasjon - bygge kultur som verdsetter kontinuerlig l&aelig;ring</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Milep&aelig;lsplan (med feiring)</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- g&aring; i takt</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- klasseromspraksis</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- mestring</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- refleksjonsprosess - ringstadbekk-krysset - nyttig og effektivt refleksjonsverkt&oslash;y</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">IKT plan for sin skole - kan ikke kopieres fra noen andre</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><b>Handlingsrom for l&aelig;ring</b></span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- sette av tid</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- felles prosjektuker</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Rektor var tydelig p&aring; at han s&aring; det som sin plikt &aring; prioritere og si nei til noe av de som ble p&aring;lagt utenfra - &quot;jeg f&aring;r heller ta kjeften etterp&aring;&quot; som han sa.</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- L&aelig;rerene f&oslash;lte dette som en stor lettelse</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><i>&quot;Jeg blir n&oslash;dt til &aring; v&aelig;re med &aring; dra lasset. jeg blir n&oslash;dt til &aring; v&aelig;re med &aring; kunne sette meg inn i det som personalet st&aring;r midt oppe i. Jeg m&aring; forst&aring; dem. Jeg m&aring; kunne sette meg inn i at en l&aelig;rer i fjerde klasse, han har ikke bare datamaskinen &aring; tenke p&aring;.&quot;</i></span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">&nbsp;</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">intervju m rektor</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><b>&Aring; l&aelig;re sammen</b></span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span></p>
<ul style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">
	<li>Teamet er grunnstrukturen i en l&aelig;rende organisasjon</li>
	<li>det som l&aelig;res jevnes ut og blir felleseie</li>
	<li>team er en gruppeferdighet<br />
		&nbsp;</li>
</ul>
<p><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><b>Mentale modeller</b></span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- Hva mener vi egentlig?</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- mye tid for &aring; snakke med l&aelig;rerene - om det som skjer i klasserommet</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- t&oslash;rre &aring; bruke elevene p&aring; en annen m&aring;te - elevene som aktive kunnskapsprodusenter</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- bryte vante forestillinger om l&aelig;ring</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">KOmpetansehevingsstrategi</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Trinn 1: Alle skal ettersp&oslash;rre - finne ut av, bli kjent med digitale ressurser innen sitt fag</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Trinn 2: &aring; kunne ta i bruk</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Trinn 3: produsere l&aelig;ringsressurser selv</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Vi m&aring;</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">&nbsp;</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><u>tenke fag</u></span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">&nbsp;</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">n&aring;r vi tenker IKT</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Tilpasset oppl&aelig;ring - sv&aelig;rt ulike niv&aring;er</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Ekstern veiledning - n&aelig;rhet mellom kompetansemilj&oslash; og skole</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><b>S4C Sosiale medier i klasserommet - Liv Marie Schou</b></span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Digitale samarbeidsverkt&oslash;y; SMS, Google docs og iEtherpad, men mest: Facebook</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Brukt i nynorsk (vgs) oppl&aelig;ring.</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Opprettet egne fagsider p&aring; Facebook. Legger ut lekser, beskjeder, lenker osv.</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />

	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Lukka gruppe for Vg1 - &aring;pen side for Vg2 og Vg3</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Hva gj&oslash;r vi p&aring; Facebook?</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- tillegg til l&aelig;ringsplattforma</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- legg ut aktuelle lenker elvene kan kommentere</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- viser til program med falgig relevans t.d. NRK</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- p&aring;stand/lenke i statsfeltet som elevene diskuterer og kommenterer</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- skriv lekser, p&aring;minninger og meldinger i statusfeltet</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- Elevene skriv korte tekster, referat og refleksjoner. 	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Egne dikt p&aring; nynorsk. &quot;Nynorskdiktet du liker&quot;.</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />

	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Korte referat. Referat f.eks. fra &quot;Tatt av kvinnen&quot;.&nbsp;</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Ord for dagen.</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Facebook - toveiskommunikasjon.</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Facebook, eleven og l&aelig;reren</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- Bruk Facebook som del av undervisninga</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- Gi oppmuntrende og postive kommentarer. Aldri irrettesettende kommentarer faglig p&aring; facebook (andre ser det).&nbsp;</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- Unng&aring; personlige tilbakemeldinger. Tilbakemeldinger gis face-to-face.</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- ver eintydig positiv</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- legg ikkje ut karakterer til elvene p&aring; Facebook</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- Vis god holdning og l&aelig;r eleven det samme (nettvett/nettikette)</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />

	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Form&aring;let med Facebook:</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- oppn&aring; en god og trivlig dialog med elevene</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- &oslash;ke og ivareta skrivegleden hos eleven</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- skriving og aktualitet h&aring;nd i h&aring;nd</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Gitt klar beskjed om at ho svarer dersom ho ser meldingane, har tid og anledning, men at dei ikkje m&aring; forvente svar.</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">SMS-time (stort sett flytta over p&aring; Facebook)</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- lyrikk p&aring; SMS (egenprodusert tekst)</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- nynorsk p&aring; sms</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- ord for dagen</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Googledokument</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">En oppretter dokumentet og inviterer andre p&aring; mail</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">- meir tungvindt enn&nbsp;</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />

	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><b>S4A del 2 - Prosjekt om digitale fortellinger p&aring; NTNU</b></span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">oppgaven studentene fikk:</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">lag en personlig fortelling om&nbsp;</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">...en forfatter eller</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">...en litter&aelig;r figur eller</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">...en leseopplevelse du har hatt</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">Lag gjerne en jeg-fortelling</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />

	</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">L&aelig;rersutdentene skulle</span><span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; "><br />
	</span></p>
<ul style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Times; font-size: medium; ">
	<li>fa erfaring med en form for digital tekstskaping (s&aring;kalt &quot;digital storytelling&quot;)</li>
	<li>utvikle sin digitale kompetanse</li>

Han vil ta oss med p&aring; fortellingen; sp&oslash;rsm&aring;l f&oslash;rst: Hvem var her i 2006. Fantastisk!
